Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Introduction to Al-Hilatul Najijah: A Hanafi Guide to Shariah-Compliant Solutions for Women's Marital Difficulties
Title page and descriptive subtitle of the book

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the purpose and scope of Al-Hilatul Najijah and explain its significance in the Hanafi tradition of legal stratagems (hiyal).

Core Idea
Al-Hilatul Najijah provides permissible Hanafi stratagems to resolve marital hardships for women.

This lesson introduces Al-Hilatul Najijah, a specialized work by Hakim al-Ummat Maulana Ashraf Ali Thanwi. The book addresses critical family law issues where women face difficulties, offering Shariah-compliant solutions within the Hanafi school. Understanding its scope helps students appreciate the role of legal stratagems (hiyal) in providing relief while maintaining Shariah boundaries.

Guided Path
1
Identify the author and his significance
The author is Hakim al-Ummat Maulana Ashraf Ali Thanwi (d. 1362 AH), a renowned Hanafi jurist and spiritual guide. His works are authoritative in the Hanafi tradition, especially in the Indian subcontinent.
Thanwi is known for his deep legal acumen and integration of tasawwuf with fiqh.
2
Understand the meaning of 'Al-Hilatul Najijah'
'Hilah' in Hanafi terminology refers to a permissible legal device to achieve a legitimate objective without violating Shariah. 'Najijah' means successful or effective. Thus, the title signifies 'The Successful Stratagem'.
Hilah is distinguished from trickery (makr) because it operates within the bounds of Shariah.
3
List the key issues addressed
The book covers: divorce rights, release from a missing husband (mafqud al-khabar), insane husband (majnun), impotent husband (innin), annulment for minors (faskh al-nikah), prohibited relations for marriage, marriage with Europeans, and Muslim Personal Law.
These are practical problems that often leave women in legal limbo.
4
Recognize the context and purpose
Thanwi wrote the book to provide a comprehensive, evidence-based manual for muftis and women facing these hardships. The subtitle emphasizes 'comprehensive researched investigations' (madlal tahqiqat).
The book is not a general fiqh manual but a specialized work for specific cases.
5
Relate to Hanafi ifta practice
Muftis use this book as a reference to issue fatwas in family law cases. The hiyal (stratagems) it contains are based on the Hanafi school's established positions and permissible methods.
Knowledge of such works is essential for a mufti to provide relief while adhering to the school.

Al-Hilatul Najijah: i.e., the Shariah solution for the problems of oppressed women. By the expert of the Hanafi school, Maulana Shah Ashraf Ali Thanwi (may Allah have mercy on him). 247554. Maktaba Radi, Dioband (India).
Al-Hilatul Najijah: i.e., rulings of divorce and the Shariah court system, which includes: rights of women regarding divorce, method of obtaining release from a missing husband, an insane husband, and an impotent husband; also annulment of marriage for a minor, prohibited marriage relations, marriage with European nations, and comprehensive researched investigations on Muslim Personal Law. By Hakim al-Ummat Maulana Shah Ashraf Ali Thanwi (may Allah have mercy on him). New arrangement facilitated by Maulana Khursheed Hasan Qasimi, companion of Dar al-Ifta, Dar al-Ulum Deoband. 247554. Radi Dioband (India).
Source pages p. 1

Commentary
This is the front matter of Al-Hilatul Najijah, a work by the eminent Hanafi jurist and spiritual guide Hakim al-Ummat Maulana Shah Ashraf Ali Thanwi (d. 1362 AH). The passage consists of the title page and a descriptive subtitle. The book addresses critical issues in family law that often leave women in difficult circumstances, particularly in the Hanafi milieu of the Indian subcontinent. It covers the Shariah rulings on divorce, the legal mechanisms for women to obtain release from a missing husband (mafqud al-khabar), a husband afflicted with insanity (majnun), or an impotent husband (innin). Additionally, it discusses the annulment of marriage (faskh) for minors, prohibited degrees in marriage (mahram), marriage with Europeans, and provides detailed research on Muslim Personal Law. The subtitle indicates that the book aims to offer comprehensive, evidence-based (madlal) solutions within the framework of Shariah. The present edition has been newly arranged by Maulana Khursheed Hasan Qasimi, who is affiliated with Dar al-Ifta at Dar al-Ulum Deoband, and published by Maktaba Radi in Dioband, India. The numbers '247554' likely refer to the book's code or printing number.

Key Terms
الحيلة الناجزة (Al-Hilatul Najijah): The book title, meaning 'The Successful Stratagem' or 'The Effective Legal Solution'—a work providing Shariah-compliant solutions for women's marital difficulties.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the primary subject of Al-Hilatul Najijah?
A) Islamic inheritance laws
B) Shariah solutions for women's marital problems
C) Business transactions and contracts
D) Criminal law and punishments

Key Takeaway
Al-Hilatul Najijah is a Hanafi guide to permissible stratagems that provide relief to women in difficult marital situations.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Introducing Al-Hilatul Najijah: The Method of Hanafi Fatwa in Difficult Cases
Title page and preface of Al-Hilatul Najijah

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the purpose and methodology of Ashraf Ali Thanwi's book Al-Hilatul Najijah, and explain how it exemplifies Hanafi fatwa practice in complex family law issues.

Core Idea
Al-Hilatul Najijah provides permissible legal stratagems (hila) for Muslim women facing marital hardship, rooted in rigorous Hanafi scholarship.

This lesson introduces the book Al-Hilatul Najijah by Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi, a landmark Hanafi work on family law. The title page and preface reveal the author's meticulous methodology: he consulted Maliki scholars in Madinah, involved multiple Hanafi institutions, and sought review from scholars across India before finalizing any ruling. This sets the stage for understanding how a Hanafi mufti approaches complex and disputed issues, especially when addressing the needs of vulnerable individuals.

Guided Path
1
Identify the book's subject
From the title page, list the main topics covered: women's rights to divorce, missing husbands, insane or impotent husbands, annulment of marriage of minors, prohibited marriage relations, marriage with Europeans, and Muslim Personal Law.
These are all areas where classical Hanafi rulings may need adaptation or special solutions (hila).
2
Recognize the author's authority
Note the honorific 'Hakim al-Ummat' given to Ashraf Ali Thanwi, indicating his status as a wise guide for the community. This adds weight to the methodology described.
Thanwi is a major figure in the Deoband tradition, which follows the Hanafi school.
3
Trace the methodology
From the preface, identify the steps: (1) personal ijtihad and mental effort, (2) correspondence with Maliki scholars in Madinah for doubts, (3) review by scholars of Darul Uloom Deoband and Madrasa Mazahir al-Uloom, (4) sending issues to other famous scholars across India for consultation, (5) incorporating all responses into the book.
This shows a collective, multi-madhhab approach while remaining within Hanafi framework.
4
Understand the term 'hila'
In this context, 'hila' refers to legitimate legal stratagems (plural: hiyal) that achieve a permissible outcome while avoiding prohibited means. It is not trickery but a recognized tool in Hanafi fiqh.
The Hanafi school is known for permitting hiyal in cases of necessity, as seen in works like Al-Hiyal by Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani.
5
Appreciate the editorial work
Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi, from the Dar al-Ifta of Darul Uloom Deoband, added new headings and simplified the text to make it more accessible. This reflects the ongoing tradition of making classical Hanafi works usable for contemporary muftis.
Dar al-Ifta is the official fatwa department, so the editor's role ensures the book meets institutional standards.

کتاب کے بارے میں
نحمده ونصلى على رسوله الكريم مسائل مندرجہ الحیلۃ الناجزة" جس قدر ضروری اور اہم تھے اس سے زیادہ میرا ہم تھا کہ اس دشوار گذار میدان میں قدم کون رکھے، دنیا و آخرت کی اتنی بڑی ذمہ داری کون اٹھائے ، اس کے لئے بے شمار کتابوں کی ورق گردانی اور علماء وقت سے مراجعت
و مشاورت کی مشقت کون برداشت کرے؟
جبکہ ہر طبقہ کے علماء میں ان مسائل پر مفصل تصنیف کی اشد ضرورت محسوس کی جاتی تھی مگر علمی دشواریاں سدراہ بن جاتی تھیں۔ اللہ تعالیٰ کو حضرت حکیم الامت نورہ اللہ مرقدہ کے دست مبارک سے یہ خدمت لینا تھی آپ کے قلب میں اس کا داعیہ قوت کے ساتھ پیدا ہوا، درحقیقت اُن ہی کی ذاتِ اقدس اس فریضہ کی متحمل ہو سکتی تھی آپ نے اپنے خدا داد و رع و تقوی کی وجہ سے صرف اپنی دماغی کاوش اور محنت و مشقت کے بعد استخراج مسائل پر اکتفانہ فرمایا؛ بلکہ جس مسئلہ میں ذرا شبہ ہوا بار بار مالکی المذہب علماء مدینہ طیبہ سے خط و کتابت کرتے رہے، پھر ام المدارس دار العلوم دیوبند اور مدرسہ مظاہر العلوم سہارنپور کے علماء کو اس تصنیف میں گو یا شریک رکھا، کتاب کا کوئی لفظ ان حضرات کی نظر و مشوروں کے بغیر نہیں لکھا گیا لیکن اس کے بعد بھی یہ ضروری سمجھا گیا کہ ہندوستان کے دوسرے علماء شاہیر سے بھی اس میں مشورہ لیا جائے ، چنانچہ تمام مشہور علماء کی خدمت میں یہ مسائل بغرض مشور ہ بھیجے گئے اور الحمد للہ ان
حضرات کے جوابات و مشورہ موصول ہوئے جو کتاب میں درج کر دئے گئے ہیں۔ نیز اللہ تعالیٰ جزائے خیر عنایت فرمائے برادر معظم مولانا خورشید حسن قاسمی رفیق دار الافتاء دار العلوم دیو بند کو کہ موصوف نے کتاب کو جدید عنوانات اور تسهیل فرما کر عام فہم کر دیا ہے، اللہ تعالٰی مزید خدمت لیتا ر ہے اور قبول بھی فرمائے ، آمین۔
طالب دعا
محمد رفعت قاسمی
خادم التدریس دار العلوم دیوبند
ار محرم الحرام ۱۴۲۶ ۲۰۷۵ فروری ۲۰۰۵ء
Al-Hilatul Najijah, meaning: Rulings of Divorce and the Islamic Legal System, in which: women's rights to divorce, the method of getting rid of a missing husband, insane or impotent husband, also annulment of marriage of a minor, prohibited marriage relations, marriage with European nations, and comprehensive evidenced investigations on Muslim Personal Law. By Hakim al-Ummat Maulana Shah Ashraf Ali Thanwi (may Allah have mercy on him). New arrangement and simplification by Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi, companion of Dar al-Ifta, Darul Uloom Deoband. [Number] 247554, [unclear] Razi wa la buddah, India.

About the book: We praise Him and send blessings on His noble Messenger. The issues included in Al-Hilatul Najijah were as necessary and important as they were, but my concern was greater: who would step into this difficult field? Who would bear such a great responsibility of this world and the Hereafter? For this, who would endure the labor of leafing through countless books and consulting with contemporary scholars?

While scholars of all classes felt the dire need for a detailed work on these issues, academic difficulties stood as obstacles. Allah Most High wanted this service from the blessed hands of Hadrat Hakim al-Ummat (may Allah illuminate his grave). A strong motivation was created in his heart. Indeed, only his sacred person could undertake this duty. Due to his God-given insight and piety, he did not content himself with merely deriving issues after his own mental effort and hard work; rather, whenever there was any doubt in a matter, he repeatedly corresponded with Maliki scholars of Madinah Tayyibah. Then he also made the scholars of the mother institution Darul Uloom Deoband and Madrasa Mazahir al-Uloom Saharanpur partners in this work. Not a single word of the book was written without their review and advice. But even after this, it was deemed necessary to also consult with other famous scholars of India. So these issues were sent to all famous scholars for consultation. Alhamdulillah, their replies and advice were received and have been recorded in the book. Also, may Allah reward brother Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi, companion of Dar al-Ifta, Darul Uloom Deoband, for he has made the book easier to understand with new headings and simplification. May Allah continue to accept further service, Ameen.

The supplicant: Muhammad Rifat Qasimi, teacher at Darul Uloom Deoband, 1 Muharram 1426 AH / 10 February 2005.
Source pages p. 2

Commentary
This passage is the front matter of the book Al-Hilatul Najijah. The title page introduces the book as a work on divorce rulings and Islamic judicial system, covering critical issues such as women's rights to divorce, missing husbands, insane or impotent husbands, annulment of marriage for minors, marriage prohibitions, marriage with Europeans, and a comprehensive evidenced study of Muslim Personal Law. The author is the renowned Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi (d. 1362 AH). The new edition has been arranged and simplified by Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi.

The preface, written by Muhammad Rifat Qasimi, explains the rigorous methodology followed by Ashraf Ali Thanwi in writing this book. Recognizing the dire need for a work addressing these complex and sensitive fiqhi issues, Thanwi undertook the task with extreme caution. He did not rely solely on his own research; whenever any issue posed a doubt, he corresponded repeatedly with Maliki scholars in Madinah to ensure accuracy. He also involved scholars from Darul Uloom Deoband and Madrasa Mazahir al-Uloom in reviewing the manuscript. Every word was written after their scrutiny. Subsequently, the issues were sent to other prominent scholars across India for consultation, and their responses are included in the book. This demonstrates the Hanafi tradition of thoroughness and reliance on collective scholarly input (shura) in issuing fatwas, especially in matters where differences between schools (ikhtilaf) arise. The preface also acknowledges Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi for simplifying the book with modern headings. This front matter sets the stage for a work that is both deeply rooted in classical Hanafi methodology and responsive to contemporary legal challenges.

Key Terms
الحيلة الناجزة (al-hilat al-najizah): The 'effective legal stratagem' — the title of the book, referring to shar'i solutions (hila) for difficult family law problems such as divorce from missing or impotent husbands.
حکیم الامت (hakim al-ummah): Title meaning 'Wise one of the nation' given to Ashraf Ali Thanwi.
دار الافتاء (dar al-ifta): The fatwa department of Darul Uloom Deoband where the editor, Khurshid Hasan Qasimi, works.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the preface, what did Ashraf Ali Thanwi do when he had doubt about a particular issue?
A) He relied solely on his own ijtihad.
B) He consulted Maliki scholars in Madinah.
C) He ignored the issue and skipped it.
D) He changed the ruling to match the majority opinion.

Key Takeaway
Ashraf Ali Thanwi's rigorous methodology in Al-Hilatul Najijah exemplifies the Hanafi tradition of thorough consultation and scholarly verification before issuing fatwas on complex family law issues.

Introduction and Front Matter
intermediate
8 min
The Scholarly Methodology Behind Al-Hilatun Najizah
Preface describing the compilation method of Al-Hilatun Najizah.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the steps of scholarly consultation (shura) used by Hakim al-Ummat in compiling Al-Hilatun Najizah and explain why each step strengthens the reliability of a fatwa.

Core Idea
A single scholar's ijtihad is verified through cross-madhhab consultation and institutional review.

This preface reveals the meticulous methodology behind Al-Hilatun Najizah. Far from a solitary effort, the author engaged Maliki scholars in Madinah, senior faculty at Darul Uloom Deoband and Mazahir Uloom, and prominent Indian scholars. Understanding this process teaches us the importance of consultation (shura) in issuing reliable fatwas.

Guided Path
1
Identify the author's initial concern
Recognise the difficulty and responsibility the author felt in writing on these issues. He worried about the vast responsibility in this world and the Hereafter.
2
Trace the consultation levels
Note the sequence: personal extraction → correspondence with Maliki scholars in Madinah → review by Darul Uloom Deoband and Mazahir Uloom scholars → final consultation with prominent Indian scholars.
Each level adds a layer of verification.
3
Understand the purpose
The purpose was to remove doubt and ensure accuracy. Whenever there was any doubt, consultation was sought. No word was written without review.
This demonstrates the principle of verification in ifta.
4
Connect to fatwa hierarchy
The resulting fatwa gains authority from the collective verification. This process elevates the work from personal opinion to a more reliable source.
Compare with the concept of 'ijma' and shura.

و مشاورت کی مشقت کون برداشت کرے؟

حضرات کے جوابات و مشورہ موصول ہوئے جو کتاب میں درج کر دئے گئے ہیں۔ نیز اللہ تعالیٰ جزائے خیر عنایت فرمائے برادر معظم مولانا خورشید حسن قاسمی رفیق دار الافتاء دار العلوم دیو بند کو کہ موصوف نے کتاب کو جدید عنوانات اور تسهیل فرما کر عام فہم کر دیا ہے، اللہ تعالٰی مزید خدمت لیتا ر ہے اور قبول بھی فرمائے ، آمین۔

محمد رفعت قاسمی

We praise Him and send blessings upon His noble Messenger. The issues included in Al-Hilatun Najizah were as necessary and important as they were, but my concern was more: who would step into this difficult field? Who would bear such a great responsibility in this world and the Hereafter? Who would endure the hardship of turning countless pages and consulting and corresponding with contemporary scholars? While scholars of every stratum felt the acute need for a detailed work on these issues, scholarly difficulties became a barrier. Allah willed that this service be taken from the blessed hand of Hakim al-Ummat (may Allah illuminate his resting place); the motivation for it arose strongly in his heart. In reality, only his noble person could bear this duty. Due to his God-given intelligence and piety, he did not suffice with mere mental exertion and hard work alone in extracting the issues; rather, whenever there was the slightest doubt in any issue, he repeatedly corresponded with Maliki scholars of Madinah Munawwarah. Then he virtually included the scholars of Darul Uloom Deoband and Madrasa Mazahir Uloom Saharanpur as partners in this work. No word of the book was written without the review and advice of these gentlemen. But even after that, it was deemed necessary to seek advice from other prominent scholars of India. Accordingly, these issues were sent to all renowned scholars for consultation, and praise be to Allah, their replies and advice were received and have been included in the book. Also, may Allah grant the best reward to our respected brother Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi, colleague at Dar al-Ifta of Darul Uloom Deoband, who has made the book accessible to the general public by adding new headings and simplifying it. May Allah continue to take more service and accept it. Ameen. Seeking prayers, Muhammad Rifat Qasimi, teacher at Darul Uloom Deoband, 1st Muharram 1426, 10th February 2005.
Source pages p. 3

Commentary
This passage is the preface authored by Muhammad Rifat Qasimi, describing the context and methodology behind the compilation of Al-Hilatun Najizah. It highlights the author's (Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi's) careful approach: he not only relied on his own scholarly extraction but actively sought verification from Maliki scholars in Madinah, incorporated input from scholars of Darul Uloom Deoband and Mazahir Uloom, and finally consulted prominent Indian scholars across the country. This underscores the principle of thoroughness and consultation (shura) in issuing fatwas and legal stratagems, a key characteristic of reliable Hanafi fiqh works. The preface also acknowledges the editorial work of Maulana Khurshid Hasan Qasimi in modernizing the book's presentation.

Key Terms
الحیلۃ الناجزہ (al-hilatun najizah): The title of the book, meaning 'The Successful Stratagem' or 'The Effective Legal Device'.
شوریٰ (shura): Consultation; the practice of seeking advice from qualified scholars before making a decision.
استخراج مسائل (istikhrāj masā’il): Extraction of rulings from primary sources.

Key Terms from Source Passage

A) To increase the number of authors credited on the book

D) To avoid writing the book himself

Key Takeaway
The compilation of Al-Hilatun Najizah exemplifies the Hanafi principle that fatwa reliability is strengthened through cross-madhhab and institutional consultation.

Core Idea
The table of contents reveals the book's focus on legal stratagems for divorce and court procedures in Hanafi fiqh.

This lesson presents the table of contents of Al-Hilat al-Najizah, a Hanafi work on legal stratagems (hiyal). While a table of contents may seem mundane, it provides a bird's-eye view of the author's concerns: delegation of divorce, conditions of a qadi, and acting upon another madhhab. As a mufti, navigating such a table is the first step in finding the right ruling for a complex case.

Guided Path
1
Scan the main headings
Identify the broad categories: preface, conditions of qadi, fatwa according to another madhhab, delegation of divorce, marriage deeds, etc.

Note the page numbers
Understand the structure and length of each section; this helps prioritize reading.
Page numbers are approximate but give a sense of the work's organization.
3
Relate topics to fatwa practice
Think how each topic is relevant to a mufti's daily work: delegating divorce, drafting marriage contracts, issuing fatwas in non-Muslim lands.
The book is a toolkit for problematic scenarios.

Phrases like 'تفویض طلاق' (delegation of divorce), 'کابین نامہ' (marriage deed), 'حیلہ ناجزہ' (the effective stratagem) are central.

If a mufti needs a ruling on a specific issue, decide which section to consult first based on keywords from the query.
Complex cases may require consulting multiple sections.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Navigating Al-Hilatul Najijah: Structure and Key Themes
Table of contents of Al-Hilatul Najijah

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the major topics covered in Al-Hilatul Najijah and locate specific discussions by page number.

Core Idea
Al-Hilatul Najijah provides practical legal solutions (hila) for marital disputes within the Hanafi school.

The table of contents (fihrist) of a fiqh book is more than a list—it is a roadmap of the author's jurisprudence. This lesson introduces you to the structure of Al-Hilatul Najijah, a concise work by Ashraf Ali Thanwi that addresses urgent marital issues using Hanafi legal solutions. By understanding the layout, you will quickly find rulings on delegation of divorce, impotence, non-Muslim magistrates, and other practical problems faced in the Indian subcontinent.

Guided Path
1
Scan the main headings
Look at the headings in the table of contents. Identify repeated terms like 'حق طلاق' (right of divorce), 'بین نامہ' (marriage deed), and 'شرعی کمیٹی' (Shari'a committee).
These indicate the book's focus on divorce delegation and dispute resolution.
2
Recognise the book's purpose
The word 'حیلہ' (hila) appears in the title. Note that this book offers 'practical solutions' within the Hanafi school, not abstract theory.
Hila are legal stratagems to achieve a permissible outcome while avoiding impermissible means.
3
Identify procedural topics
Look for headings on 'قاضی' (qadi), 'مجسٹریٹ' (magistrate), and 'فیصلہ' (decision). These show the book's concern with court procedures, especially in non-Muslim majority contexts.
This is crucial for iftaa in modern secular states.
4
Note cross-madhhab references
Headings like 'ضرورة دوسرے امام کی اتباع' (following another imam out of necessity) indicate that the author sometimes invokes non-Hanafi positions when necessity demands.
This reflects the Hanafi principle of 'al-darura' allowing temporary departure from the school.

Commentary
This passage is a table of contents (fihrist) for the book Al-Hilatul Najijah. It lists chapter titles and corresponding page numbers, covering topics such as marriage contracts (kabin nama), delegation of divorce (tafwid al-talaq), suspended divorce (ta'liq al-talaq), procedures in non-Muslim countries, rulings of qadis and magistrates, impotence (injin), necessity to follow another imam, conditions for a mufti, and guidance for Shari'a committees. The pages serve as a roadmap to the book's legal discussions, which are primarily concerned with practical solutions (hila) for marital issues within the Hanafi school.

Key Terms
کابین نامہ (kābin nāmah): Marriage deed or marriage contract document
تفویض طلاق (tafwīḍ al-ṭalāq): Delegation of the right to divorce to the wife
تعلیق طلاق (taʿlīq al-ṭalāq): Suspended divorce – making divorce conditional upon a future event
عنین (ʿanīn): Impotent man; one unable to perform sexual intercourse
شرعی کمیٹی (sharʿī kamīṭī): Shari'a committee – a body of scholars that adjudicates according to Islamic law

Key Terms from Source Passage

Al-Hilatul Najijah's table of contents reveals a practical, problem-oriented fiqh work focused on marital solutions across different legal contexts.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner

Orientation to Al-Hilatul Najijah: A Mufti's Reference on Marriage Annulments
Index listing topics and page numbers

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to navigate the table of contents of Al-Hilatul Najijah to locate key sections on impotence (عنین) and madness (مجنون) and explain the book's utility for fatwa-giving.

Core Idea
Al-Hilatul Najijah is a mufti's toolkit for resolving marriage crises through Hanafi legal stratagems.

This lesson introduces the table of contents of Al-Hilatul Najijah by Ashraf Ali Thanwi, a key text on legal stratagems (hiyal) in Hanafi law. As a mufti, you will often encounter cases of marital discord due to impotence or madness. This table of contents shows how the book systematically addresses these issues, from definitions to procedural solutions. Understanding this structure is your first step toward effective fatwa-writing in such cases.

Guided Path
1
Scan the table for key themes
Identify the major topics: impotence (عنین), madness (مجنون), sharia committees, and following other madhhabs. Notice the page numbers to gauge the depth of coverage.
2
Locate the section on impotence (عنین)
Find entries like 'عنین کی تعریف' (definition) and 'نامرد کی بیوی کی تفریق' (separation of the impotent's wife). Note the page range (e.g., 26–90) to see the extensive treatment.
The definition appears on page 26.
3
Locate the section on madness (مجنون)
Find 'مجنون کی بیوی کا تفریق' and related entries. Observe that madness is covered from page 91 onward, with distinct sub-topics like temporary vs. permanent insanity.
4
Identify references to other madhhabs
Note pages that mention 'مذہب مالکیہ' (Maliki school) and 'دیگر مذہب پر عمل' (acting on other madhhabs). This shows the book's practical approach using ikhtilaf as a mercy.
For example, pages 73 and 90 discuss Maliki rulings on treatment period.
5
Understand the book's arrangement
Recognize the progression from definitions to proofs to procedures. This reflects the mufti's workflow: understand the issue, evaluate evidence, then issue a ruling.

Table of Contents: Page numbers and headings: The legal status of the arrangement of the sharia committee; If a Muslim magistrate is not available; Participation of scholars in the sharia committee; Neglect of wife's rights; Sharia committee's authority; Divorce from a recalcitrant husband; Permissibility in times of severe necessity; Dissenting decisions not accepted; Majority decision; Urging not to abandon one's madhhab; Separation of the wife of an impotent man; Conditions for the mufti; The saved sect and the elders of India; Definition of the impotent man; Payment for Quran recitation; Clarification of the juristic definition of impotence; Acting on another imam's madhhab due to necessity; Regarding the wife's examination; More discussion on following another madhhab; Payment for teaching fiqh; Acting on the Maliki book Tadwinah; Guiding principles for the sharia committee; Duration of treatment for eye illness based on moon calculation; Method for separation of the wife of a madman; Discussion on annulment if no improvement in a year; Opinions of imams regarding the wife of a madman; Types of madness: permanent and temporary; Duration of treatment for impotence in Maliki school; Condition for annulment for the impotent; Ruling on dangerous madman; Wife's right to annulment after the impotent's one-year treatment; Wife's iddah and mahr; Imam Muhammad's view on the wife of a madman; Examination of the impotent's genitals; Maliki and Hanafi agreement on separation; Issue of consistency; If the madman has intercourse.
Source pages p. 6

Commentary
This passage is a table of contents (عنوانات) for the book Al-Hilatul Najijah by Ashraf Ali Thanwi. It lists various topics covered in the book along with their page numbers. The index includes chapters on legal stratagems (حیل), marriage and divorce issues, particularly cases involving impotence (عنین), madness (جنون), and the role of a sharia committee. It also touches upon conditions for a mufti, following another madhhab under necessity, and procedural guidelines. The page numbers are in both Arabic and Western numerals. This front matter serves as a reference guide for the reader.

Key Terms
عنوانات (unwanat): Table of contents or headings
عنین (‘innin): An impotent man, unable to perform intercourse
مجنون (majnoon): A person suffering from insanity or mental disorder

Key Terms from Source Passage

Key Takeaway
The table of contents of Al-Hilatul Najijah is a map of Hanafi legal stratagems for marriage crises, guiding the mufti from definition to solution.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Navigating the Table of Contents: Key Family Law Issues in Hanafi Fiqh
Table of contents listing chapter headings and page numbers for three family law topics

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the three main family law topics covered in this Hanafi text and locate their page references in the table of contents.

Core Idea
The table of contents maps the structured treatment of impotence, insanity, and missing husband in Hanafi fiqh.

This lesson introduces the table of contents of Al-Hilatul Najijah, a Hanafi work addressing critical family law issues. The TOC reveals how the book systematically covers impotence (عنین), insanity (جنون), and missing husband (مفقود), along with comparisons to the Maliki school. Understanding this structure helps you navigate the detailed rulings that follow.

Guided Path
1
Identify the three major topics
Scan the TOC for the main headings. They are عنین (impotence), مجنون (insanity), and مفقود (missing husband). Each topic spans multiple pages with sub-entries.
These are the core issues discussed in the book.
2
Note the page ranges for each topic
Look at the page numbers next to each heading. For example, impotence starts around page 84 and continues to page 90. Insanity appears from page 92 to 105. Missing husband is covered from page 114 to 123.
Some pages may be shared between topics.
3
Recognize subtopics within each issue
Under each main heading, you'll find sub-entries like duration of treatment, conditions for annulment, waiting period, and more. For instance, under عنین there is 'مدت علاج' (treatment duration) on page 91.
These subtopics help you quickly locate detailed rulings.
4
Observe inter-madhhab comparisons
Note the entries that mention 'مالکیہ' or 'مالکی', indicating comparison with the Maliki school. Examples include page 90 and 108. This shows the book engages with other madhhabs.
Such comparisons are valuable for a mufti dealing with complex cases.
5
Understand the TOC's pedagogical purpose
The TOC is not just an index; it reflects the book's method: each issue is broken down into causes, treatments, legal consequences, and procedural steps. This structure aids systematic learning and reference.
Use this TOC as a roadmap when studying or issuing fatwas.

Commentary
This passage is the table of contents (عناوین) of the book Al-Hilatul Najijah. It lists the major topics and their page numbers. The book appears to cover Hanafi legal rulings on three main issues: impotence (عنین), insanity (جنون), and missing husband (مفقود). For each issue, the table details conditions, treatments, waiting periods, and procedures for annulment of marriage, as well as comparisons with the Maliki school. The presence of page numbers like 91-123 suggests a significant portion of the book is devoted to these family law problems. This front matter gives the reader an overview of the structured treatment of these topics within the Hanafi madhhab.

Key Terms
عنین (‘innīn): A man who is impotent, unable to have intercourse with his wife.
مجنون (majnūn): An insane person, one who is not legally accountable.
مفقود (mafqūd): A missing person, one whose whereabouts are unknown.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Navigating the Table of Contents of Al-Hilatul Najijah
Front matter – table of contents for fatwa collection

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to locate specific fatwa chapters in Al-Hilatul Najijah using its table of contents and identify the main topics covered.

Core Idea
A table of contents is the key to unlocking the book's systematic treatment of missing-person cases.

Al-Hilatul Najijah is a collection of fatwas and solutions for complex marital disputes, especially those involving missing husbands (mafqud) and insane husbands. The table of contents (عنوانات) on pages 12-13 lists all chapters and their starting pages, allowing the mufti to quickly find relevant rulings. This lesson will guide you through reading this TOC despite OCR imperfections.

Guided Path
1
Identify the structure
Note the two-page layout: page 12 lists topics starting from page 11, and page 13 continues with additional topics. The TOC uses Arabic/Urdu headings with page numbers in Eastern Arabic digits.
OCR errors may misplace numbers; verify against original if possible.
2
Locate key topics
Scan for repeated terms like 'مفقود' (missing person), 'زوجہ' (wife), and 'مجنون' (insane). These indicate the main legal issues addressed. For example, 'بابت مفقود' means 'regarding the missing person'.
Ignore garbled words like 'لاپر واہ' – focus on recognisable fiqh terms.
3
Use page numbers
Each entry ends with a number in parentheses or after a space, e.g. '۲۷۱'. This is the starting page for that topic. When studying a specific case, turn directly to that page.
Numbers are in Eastern Arabic (e.g. ۲۷۱ = 271). Some numbers may be missing due to OCR.
4
Recognise repeated entries
Notice multiple entries for similar topics (e.g., 'زوجہ مفقود' appears several times). These are sub-sections or different fatwas. The TOC provides an overview of the book's comprehensive coverage.
The book contains fatwas from multiple scholars; each entry may be a separate response.

Commentary
This passage is the table of contents (عنوانات) for Al-Hilatul Najijah, covering pages 12-13. It lists the legal issues and topics discussed in the book, focusing on problems related to missing husbands (مفقود), wives of missing persons, wives of insane husbands (زوجہ مجنون), and the role of judges and Shari'i committees. The page numbers indicate where each topic begins. While the OCR is noisy, the structure shows the book's systematic approach to these legal dilemmas, often providing Hanafi-based solutions (hilal) and references to fatwas from scholars of Madinah and elsewhere. This front matter helps students navigate the book's content.

Key Terms
مفقود الخبر (mafqud al-khabar): A person whose news is unknown; a missing person whose whereabouts are unknown and no news of life or death.
زوجہ مجنون (zawja majnun): Wife of an insane husband; the husband's insanity is a ground for annulment of marriage under certain conditions.
شرعی کمیٹی (shar'i committee): A committee of scholars appointed to adjudicate complex marital disputes, especially in the absence of a Muslim judge.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Navigating the Table of Contents: A Gateway to Hanafi Family Law
Table of contents from a Hanafi family law manual.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the major family law topics covered in a Hanafi fiqh text and locate relevant chapters using the table of contents.

Core Idea
A well-structured table of contents is the roadmap to efficient fatwa research.

The table of contents (عنوانات) of a classical Hanafi fiqh work is not merely a list; it is a curated index of the author's legal priorities. In this lesson, we examine the TOC from 'Al-Hilat al-Najijah' by Ashraf Ali Thanwi, a text focused on legal stratagems (ḥiyal) and family law rulings. Understanding how to navigate such a TOC equips the mufti with the ability to locate rulings on marriage annulment, missing persons, and rebellious husbands swiftly.

Guided Path
1
Identify structural elements
Notice the repeated word 'عنوانات' and the page numbers. This indicates that each section is a chapter heading with its starting page.
The TOC is organized sequentially, not alphabetically.
2
Distinguish main headings from subheadings
Look for indentations or numbering (e.g., 271, 272). Main topics often have broader scope, while subheadings detail specific aspects.
Some entries are separated by blank lines or numbers.
3
Extract key legal topics
Scan for recurring themes: marriage (نكاح), divorce (طلاق), missing person (مفقود), insanity (جنون), rebellion (سركش).
The TOC covers a wide range of family law issues.
4
Map topics to fiqh chapters
Associate each topic with its likely chapter in Hanafi fiqh, such as 'book of marriage' or 'book of divorce'.
This helps in cross-referencing with other classical texts.
5
Infer the methodological approach
Terms like 'تلفيق' (talfiq) indicate discussion of combining rulings from different schools, a hallmark of Thanwi's work.
This shows the author's practical orientation for fatwa.

Commentary
These two pages constitute the table of contents (عنوانات) of the book 'Al-Hilat al-Najijah' by Ashraf Ali Thanwi. The chapters listed cover a wide range of family law and fiqh issues, particularly focusing on marriage (nikah), divorce (talaq), annulment (faskh), and rulings concerning missing persons (mafqud), insane persons (majnun), and rebellious husbands (sar-kash). The table of contents indicates that the book deals with procedural rules for Islamic courts, conditions for legal stratagems (hila), and the role of judges (qadi) and representatives (na'ib). This front matter is typical of classical fiqh works, where the table of contents serves as a roadmap for the reader. The presence of page numbers and cross-references suggests that the book is well-organized for practical fatwa issuance. As this is only a table of contents, no substantive legal rulings are extracted in this lesson.

Key Terms
عنوانات (ʿunwānāt): Table of contents, list of chapter headings
مفقود (mafqūd): A person who is missing and whose whereabouts are unknown for an extended period.
فسخ نکاح (faskh al-nikāḥ): Annulment of marriage by judicial decree due to a defect or impossibility.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Key Takeaway

Navigating the Table of Contents: The Map of Al-Hilatul Najijah
Table of contents listing topics and page numbers

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to locate key topics and page references in the table of contents of a Hanafi fatwa collection.

Core Idea
A table of contents is a roadmap for finding rulings efficiently in a Hanafi fatwa collection.

This lesson examines the table of contents (عنوانات) of Ashraf Ali Thanwi's Al-Hilatul Najijah. While tables of contents may seem trivial, understanding how a Hanafi scholar organizes a fatwa collection—by topic, by scholar, by legal procedure—is essential for efficient research. This table of contents lists entries on the missing person (mafqud), fatwas from Balkh, certifications from elders, and sample legal documents, revealing the practical scope of the work.

Guided Path
1
Identify the main topic
The central theme is the issue of the missing person (mafqud al-khabr). Locate which page numbers are dedicated to this topic.
Look for the term 'مفقود' or 'مفقود الخبر' in the TOC.
2
Scan for subtopics
Look for key nouns like 'تصدیقات' (certifications), 'فقہی عبارت' (fiqhi passages), 'نمونه' (samples). Note the diversity of sources (scholars from Balkh, Deoband, etc.).
3
Analyze the structure
The TOC is divided into two columns with page numbers. Observe that page numbers may appear as 'صفحه' followed by digits. Check for consistent formatting.
Page numbers are in Arabic-Indic numerals.
4
Connect entries to content
For each major heading, anticipate what type of ruling or discussion will be found (fatwa, certification, sample document).
For example, 'تصدیقات اکابرین' suggests endorsements from senior scholars.
5
Assess the breadth
Note the geographical range of scholars and the inclusion of procedural documents (mukhtar nama, application) under Government of India law, showing the book's modern context.

Introduction and Front Matter
intermediate
8 min
The Mufti's Role in Societal Crises: The Context of Al-Hilat al-Najizah
Author explains the historical need for his book.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the societal factors that necessitate the use of legal stratagems (hiyal) in iftaa and explain how a mufti should respond to such crises.

Core Idea
When social emergencies threaten faith, the mufti may employ permissible hiyal to prevent apostasy.

This preface of Al-Hilat al-Najizah reveals a critical juncture in 19th-century India where marital hardships pushed women toward apostasy. The author, Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi, recognized that established Hanafi rulings left many women trapped. In response, he compiled a collection of solutions from the Maliki school, permissible under the principle of necessity (darurah). This lesson explores the mufti's responsibility to assess communal crises and deploy the tool of tatabbu' al-madhahib within the bounds of Usul al-Iftaa.

Guided Path
1
Identify the societal problem described in the text.
Read the passage and pinpoint the specific hardships women faced: missing husbands, insanity, impotence, etc. What effect did these have on the community? The text says it led to the 'fitna of apostasy spreading among women.'
The problem is not just individual suffering but a collective danger to faith.
2
Analyze the mufti's response to the crisis.
How did Thanwi respond? He did not change Hanafi fiqh but sought solutions from the Maliki school. Note the process: correspondence with Madinah scholars, then presenting to muftis for discussion and scrutiny.
This is an example of tatabbu' al-madhahib (following another madhhab in necessity).
3
Extract the principles governing this response from Usul al-Iftaa.
From this narrative, derive the conditions: genuine necessity, consultation with qualified scholars, and adherence to the framework of the mufti's own madhhab. The response is permissible only as a remedy for a dire situation, not as a general rule.
This aligns with the maxim 'al-darurah tuqaddar bi qadariha' (necessity is measured by its extent).

Source Text

پیش لفظ
الحمد اللہ طویل جدوجہد کے بعد شرعی عدالت اور طلاق دنکاح کے فقہی احکام یعنی الحیلة الناجزہ کی جدید ترتیب اور جدید عنوانات کا کام مکمل ہو گیا اور کتاب منظر عام پر آگئی۔
یہ ایک تاریخی حقیقت ہے کہ آج سے تقریباً ساٹھ سال قبل شوہروں کے مظالم سے تنگ آگرہ اور شوہر کے مفقود الخبر "مجنون" عنین وغیہ صورتوں میں بیویوں کے معلق رہنے اور خواتین پر مختلف زیادیتوں کے عام ہو جانے کی وجہ سے عورتوں میں فتنہ ارتداد پھیلنا شروع ہو گیا تھا۔
اس ضرورت شدیدہ اور وقت کے اہم تقاضہ کے پیش نظر حکیم الامت " مجد د ملت حضرت تھانوی نور اللہ مرقدہ نے " الحيلة الناجزه " نامی کتاب تصنیف فرمائی۔
اور مالکی مذہب کے مدینہ منورہ سے متعدد مرتبہ مراسلات کے بعد ایسے تحادی جمع فرمائے کہ ضرورت شدیدہ میں جن پر عمل کر کے حنفی المسلک کے لیے گنجائش ہے مذکورہ موضوع پر مشتمل فتاوی کو حکیم الامت حضرت مولانا اشرف علی تھانوی صاحب نے اپنے زمانہ کے مفتیان کرام اور علماء عظام کی خدمت میں پیش فرما کہ مذاکرہ اور بحث و تنقیح کے بعد" الحملة الناجزة نامی کتاب تصنیف فرمائی اور جس کی تصنیف میں جدی المکرم حضرت مولانا مفتی محمد شفیع صاحب اور حضرت مولانا عبد الکریم صاحب گنگھوی نے غیرمعمولی
Preface. All praise to Allah, after lengthy struggle, the work of the new arrangement and new titles of the Shariah court and the fiqh rulings of divorce and marriage, i.e. Al-Hilat al-Najizah, has been completed and the book has come to public view. It is a historical fact that approximately sixty years ago, due to being distressed by the oppression of husbands and the suspension of wives in cases of missing husband, insane, impotent etc., and the prevalence of various excesses against women, the fitna of apostasy began to spread among women. In view of this severe need and the important requirement of the time, Hakim al-Ummat, Mujaddid al-Millat, Hadhrat Thanwi (may Allah illuminate his grave) authored a book named 'Al-Hilat al-Najizah'. And after multiple correspondences with the Maliki school from Madinah Munawwarah, he collected such solutions that in severe necessity, by acting upon them, there is scope for the Hanafi follower. The fatwas on the mentioned subject were presented by Hakim al-Ummat Hadhrat Mawlana Ashraf Ali Thanwi to the honorable muftis and great scholars of his time, and after discussion and scrutiny, he authored the book 'Al-Hilat al-Najizah', and in its authorship, his eminence Hadhrat Mawlana Mufti Muhammad Shafi and Hadhrat Mawlana Abdul Karim Gangohi took extraordinary [part].
Source pages p. 17

Commentary
This passage is the preface of the book. It explains the motivation behind the work: widespread marital distress among Muslim women in British India, including cases of missing husbands, insanity, impotence, and other hardships that left women in limbo. This led to a risk of apostasy. To address this, Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi compiled Al-Hilat al-Najizah, a collection of legal stratagems (hiyal) that allow Hanafi followers to adopt solutions from the Maliki school in dire necessity. The work was done after consultation with contemporary scholars and muftis, including Mufti Muhammad Shafi and Abdul Karim Gangohi.

Key Terms
الحيلة الناجزة (al-Hilat al-Najizah): The title of the book, meaning 'the successful stratagem' – a collection of legal solutions for marital problems.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What was the primary reason for writing Al-Hilat al-Najizah?
A) To teach Hanafi fiqh in a new style
B) To address the spread of apostasy among women due to marital hardships
C) To compile fatwas of Maliki scholars
D) To create a new madhhab

Key Takeaway
A mufti may use hiyal from other madhahib in dire necessity, but only after thorough consultation and scholarly scrutiny.

Tatabbu' al-Madhahib: Crossing Madhhab Boundaries in Necessity
Author describes the scholarly collaboration behind the book.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the conditions and procedure for a Hanafi mufti to adopt a ruling from another madhhab, as exemplified by the compilation of Al-Hilat al-Najizah.

Core Idea
Tatabbu' al-madhahib is permissible only under dire necessity, with consultation and scholarly oversight.

In the preface, we learn that Thanwi corresponded with Maliki scholars in Madinah and then presented the collected fatwas to contemporary muftis for discussion and approval. This lesson unpacks the usul al-iftaa methodology behind this process, focusing on the conditions, limitations, and ethical considerations of employing tatabbu' al-madhahib.

Guided Path
1
Identify the source of the adopted rulings.
The text states that Thanwi corresponded with the Maliki school from Madinah and collected solutions. This means the source of the rulings is not Hanafi but Maliki.
Recognize that this is an exception, not the norm.
2
Analyze the procedure followed.
The collected fatwas were presented to muftis and scholars for discussion and scrutiny (mudhakara wa bahth wa tanqih). This shows the importance of collective ijtihad and scholarly consensus.
The procedure ensures that the adopted rulings are properly vetted and do not contradict Islamic principles.
3
Extract the conditions for tatabbu' al-madhahib from this example.
Conditions include: severe necessity (darurah), staying within the bounds of a recognized madhhab (Maliki), and obtaining approval from contemporary scholars. The book is not a free license to shop for rulings but a structured remedy.
This aligns with the principles of Usul al-Iftaa: the mufti must avoid talfiq and ensure consistency.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner

Historical Context and Editorial Approach of Al-Hilatun Najizah
Preface describing historical context and editorial work

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the historical necessity that led Hakim al-Ummat Thanwi to compile Al-Hilatun Najizah and identify the editorial improvements introduced in this edition.

Core Idea
Al-Hilatun Najizah provides Maliki-based legal stratagems to save Hanafi women trapped by missing, insane, or impotent husbands.

Every great work of fiqh arises from a pressing need. This preface by the editor of the new edition sets the stage: a wave of apostasy among Muslim women due to oppressive marriages, with no legal exit under strict Hanafi rules. Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi responded by compiling a book of legal stratagems (hiyal) derived from Maliki sources, allowing Hanafis to adopt them in dire necessity. This lesson unpacks that historical moment and the careful editorial work done to make the text accessible today.

Guided Path
1
Recognize the crisis
Identify the social problem that motivated the book: women trapped in marriages with missing, insane, or impotent husbands, leading to apostasy.
2
Identify the solution
Note that Hakim al-Ummat Thanwi authored Al-Hilatun Najizah to provide legal stratagems from the Maliki school that Hanafis could use in such emergencies.
3
Examine the methodology
Understand that the work was done through correspondence with Maliki muftis in Medina, and the opinions were then discussed with Hanafi scholars of the time.
4
List the editorial improvements
The new edition added titles, simplified terms (preserving original meaning), reorganized long footnotes into independent articles, and translated Arabic footnotes into Urdu.
5
Appreciate the significance for iftaa
This preface shows how a mufti can resort to another madhhab in cases of dire need (darura) when the Hanafi position leads to hardship, a key principle in usul al-iftaa.

الحمد للہ طویل جدوجہد کے بعد شرعی عدالت اور طلاق و نکاح کے فقہی احکام یعنی الحیلۃ الناجزہ کی جدید ترتیب اور جدید عنوانات کا کام مکمل ہو گیا اور کتاب منظر عام پر آگئی۔

یہ ایک تاریخی حقیقت ہے کہ آج سے تقریباً ساٹھ سال قبل شوہروں کے مظالم سے تنگ آکر اور شوہر کے مفقود الخبر، مجنون، عنین وغیرہ صورتوں میں بیویوں کے معلق رہنے اور خواتین پر مختلف زیادتیوں کے عام ہو جانے کی وجہ سے عورتوں میں فتنہ ارتداد پھیلنا شروع ہو گیا تھا۔

اس ضرورت شدیدہ اور وقت کے اہم تقاضہ کے پیش نظر حکیم الامت مجدد ملت حضرت تھانوی نور اللہ مرقدہ نے "الحیلۃ الناجزہ" نامی کتاب تصنیف فرمائی۔

اور مالکی مذہب کے مدینہ منورہ سے متعدد مرتبہ مراسلات کے بعد ایسے تحادی جمع فرمائے کہ ضرورت شدیدہ میں جن پر عمل کر کے حنفی المسلک کے لیے گنجائش ہے مذکورہ موضوع پر مشتمل فتاوی کو حکیم الامت حضرت مولانا اشرف علی تھانوی صاحب نے اپنے زمانہ کے مفتیان کرام اور علماء عظام کی خدمت میں پیش فرما کر مذاکرہ اور بحث و تنقیح کے بعد "الحیلۃ الناجزہ" نامی کتاب تصنیف فرمائی اور جس کی تصنیف میں جدی المکرم حضرت مولانا مفتی محمد شفیع صاحب اور حضرت مولانا عبد الکریم صاحب گنگھوی نے غیرمعمولی تعاون فرمایا اور مدینہ منورہ کے مفتیان کرام سے فتاوی حاصل کرنے اور خط و کتابت کے سلسلہ میں شیخ الاسلام حضرت مولانا سید حسین احمد صاحب مدنی نور اللہ مرقدہ نے بھی غیر معمولی رہنمائی فرمائی۔ اگر چہ اس کتاب کے متعدد ایڈیشن شائع ہوتے رہے لیکن کتاب کے ظاہری حسن اور کتاب کے جدید عنوانات کی طرف خاطر خواہ توجہ نہیں ہو سکی، چنانچہ راقم الحروف نے حضرت کی عبارات کو باقی رکھتے ہوئے بعض جگہ معمولی طور پر تسہیل کی اور پوری کتاب پر جدید عنوانات قائم کیے اور اس سلسلہ میں مندرجہ ذیل خدمات انجام دیں۔

(۱) الحیلۃ الناجزہ کے قدیم نسخہ کی پوری کتاب کی عبارات پر جدید عنوانات پوری طرح قائم کر کے فہرست مضامین اور فہرست عنوانات کی تیاری میں شریک اشاعت کی۔ (۲) اصل کتاب کی سابقہ عبارات کو باقی رکھتے ہوئے بعض اصطلاحی الفاظ کی تسہیل کی ہے اور جن مقامات پر نمایاں تسہیل کی ہے ان کو بین القوسین کر دیا ہے لیکن حضرت کے اصل مفہوم کو پوری طرح باقی رکھا گیا ہے۔ (۳) قدیم نسخہ میں بعض مقامات پر حاشیہ نہایت طویل بلکہ کئی کئی صفحات پر مشتمل تھا جو مستقل ایک مضمون جدید عنوان قائم کر کے متعلقہ مضمون کے آخر میں پیش کر دیا گیا ہے اور ایسے مقامات پر مختصر نوٹ حاشیہ پر دے دیا گیا ہے تاکہ اس ترتیب جدید کی وضاحت ہو سکے۔ (۴) سابقہ نسخہ میں جن مقامات پر مختصر حاشیہ تھا اس کو باقی رکھتے ہوئے بعض جگہ اس کا عنوان حاشیہ پر قائم کر دیا ہے اور بعض جگہ اگر حاشیہ عربی میں تھا تو اس کا مفہوم اردو میں پیش کر دیا ہے۔
Praise be to Allah. After a long struggle, the work of new arrangement and new titles of the juristic rulings of Islamic court and divorce and marriage, i.e., al-Hilat al-Najizah, has been completed and the book has come to light. It is a historical fact that about sixty years ago, due to being fed up with the oppression of husbands and due to the suspension of wives in cases of missing, insane, impotent, etc. husbands, and the prevalence of various excesses against women, the fitna of apostasy began to spread among women. In view of this severe necessity and the important demand of the time, Hakim al-Ummat Mujaddid al-Millat Hazrat Thanwi (may Allah illuminate his grave) authored a book named "al-Hilat al-Najizah". And after multiple correspondences with the Maliki school from Medina Munawwara, he collected such legal stratagems that, in times of dire need, acting upon them provides leeway for the Hanafi school. Hazrat Maulana Ashraf Ali Thanwi presented the fatwas contained on the mentioned subject to the honorable muftis and great scholars of his time, and after discussion and scrutiny, he authored the book "al-Hilat al-Najizah". In its authorship, my honorable grandfather Hazrat Maulana Mufti Muhammad Shafi and Hazrat Maulana Abdul Karim Gangohi provided extraordinary cooperation, and in obtaining fatwas from the honorable muftis of Medina Munawwara and in correspondence, Shaykh al-Islam Hazrat Maulana Syed Husain Ahmad Madani (may Allah illuminate his grave) also provided extraordinary guidance. Although many editions of this book were published, due attention was not paid to the external beauty and new titles of the book. Therefore, the writer, while preserving the expressions of Hazrat, made ordinary simplification at some places and established new titles on the whole book, and performed the following services in this regard: (1) After establishing new titles on the expressions of the whole book of the old copy of al-Hilat al-Najizah, participated in the publication of the table of contents and the list of titles. (2) While preserving the previous expressions of the original book, simplified some technical terms, and the places where notable simplification was made have been placed in brackets, but the original meaning of Hazrat has been fully preserved. (3) In the old copy, in some places, the footnote was very long, spanning many pages, so it has been presented as an independent article with a new title at the end of the relevant article, and a short note has been given in the footnote in such places so that this new arrangement may be clarified. (4) In the previous copy, where there was a short footnote, it has been preserved, and at some places its title has been established in the footnote, and at some places if the footnote was in Arabic, its meaning has been presented in Urdu.
Source pages p. 18

Commentary
This passage is the author's preface (pesh lafz) to the new edition of Al-Hilatun Najizah. It begins by stating that the book has been republished with new arrangement and titles. The historical context is then provided: about sixty years before the time of writing (late 19th/early 20th century), many women were trapped in marriages with missing, insane, or impotent husbands, leading to a tendency toward apostasy. To address this crisis, Hakim al-Ummat Ashraf Ali Thanwi compiled this work after consulting Maliki scholars in Medina. The book provides legal stratagems (hiyal) that Hanafis can adopt in cases of dire necessity. The preface then acknowledges the contributions of Mufti Muhammad Shafi, Abdul Karim Gangohi, and Syed Husain Ahmad Madani. Finally, it details the editorial improvements: adding modern titles, simplifying terms, and reorganizing lengthy footnotes into independent articles. This preface serves to establish the book's purpose and the methodological approach taken.

Key Terms
الحیلۃ الناجزہ (al-Hilatun Najizah): Title of the book, meaning 'the effective legal stratagem'
تسہیل (tashil): Simplification of technical terms in the text for easier understanding
ضرورت شدیدہ (darura shadida): Dire necessity, a condition that permits resorting to dispensations or other madhhabs

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What was the primary reason Hakim al-Ummat Thanwi compiled Al-Hilatun Najizah?
A) To reconcile differences between Hanafi and Maliki schools.
B) To provide legal relief for Hanafi women trapped in marriages due to missing, insane, or impotent husbands.
C) To reform the Hanafi school of thought.
D) To gather Maliki fatwas for general use.

Key Takeaway
Al-Hilatun Najizah is a landmark work in Hanafi iftaa, demonstrating the use of another madhhab's rulings under the principle of darura to prevent greater harm.

Editorial Methodology in Preserving Fiqh Texts
Describes editorial modifications to the original text

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the key editorial principles used in revising a classical Hanafi fiqh text and evaluate their importance for the reliability of fatwa transmission.

Core Idea
Faithful editing preserves the author's intent while enhancing accessibility.

The editor's preface to Al-Hilatul Najijah outlines careful revisions that maintain the original meaning while improving clarity. This lesson examines these editorial choices as a model for preserving the integrity of fiqh texts in modern publication, linking to usul al-iftaa principles of reliable transmission.

Guided Path
1
Identify the editorial principles
List all the changes the editor made: adding modern headings, simplifying technical terms, relocating lengthy notes, translating Arabic margins, etc.
Refer to the 8 points in the passage.
2
Analyze the balance
Examine how the editor preserves the original meaning while making the text more accessible. Consider the use of parentheses and keeping old names alongside new ones.
This reflects the Hanafi principle of not altering the core ruling (hukm).
3
Relate to usul al-iftaa
Connect the editorial choices to principles of fatwa compilation: ensuring textual reliability (zahir al-riwayah), clarity for the mufti, and proper attribution.
The editor maintains the original authority of the text.
4
Evaluate the importance
Consider what could go wrong if editorial principles are not followed: loss of original meaning, confusion in fatwa, or misattribution.
This highlights the ethical responsibility of the mufti/editor.

تعاون فرمایا اور مدینہ منورہ کے مفتیان کرام سے فتاوی حاصل کرنے اور خط و کتابت کے سلسلہ میں شیخ الاسلام حضرت مولانا سید حسین احمد صاحب مدنی نور کہ مرقدہ نے بھی غیر معمولی رہنمائی فرمائی ۔ اگر چہ اس کتاب کے متعدد ایڈیشن شائع ہوتے رہے لیکن کتاب کے ظاہری حسن اور کتاب کے جدید عنوانات کی طرف خاطر خواہ توجہ نہیں ہوسکی، چنانچہ راقم الحروف نے حضرت کی عبارات کو باقی رکھتے ہوئے بعض جگہ معمولی طور پر تسہیل کی اور پوری کتاب پر جدید عنوانات قائم کیئے اور اس سلسلہ میں مندرجہ ذیل خدمات انجام دیں ۔

(۱) المجلة الناجزہ کے قدیم نسخہ کی پوری کتاب کی عبارات پر جدید عنوانات قائم کر کے فہرست مضامین اور فہرست عنوانات مرتب کر کے شائع کی ۔
(۲) اصل کتاب کی سابقہ عبارات کو باقی رکھتے ہوئے بعض اصطلاحی الفاظ کی تسہیل کی ہے اور جن مقامات پر نمایاں تسہیل کی ہے ان کو بین القوسین کر دیا ہے لیکن حضرت کے اصل مفہوم کو پوری طرح باقی رکھا گیا ہے۔
(۳) قدیم نسخہ میں بعض مقامات پر حاشیہ نہایت طویل بلکہ کئی کئی صفحات پر مشتمل تھا جو مستقل ایک مضمون جدید عنوان قائم کر کے متعلقہ مضمون کے آخیر میں پیش کر دیا گیا ہے اور ایسے مقامات پر مختصر نوٹ حاشیہ پر دے دیا گیا ہے تاکہ اس ترتیب جدید کی وضاحت ہو سکے۔
(۴) سابقہ نسخہ میں جن مقامات پر مختصر حاشیہ تھا اس کو باقی رکھتے ہوئے بعض جگہ اس کا عنوان حاشیہ پر قائم کر دیا ہے اور بعض جگہ اگر حاشیہ عربی میں تھا تو اس کا مفہوم اردو میں پیش کر دیا ہے ۔

(۵) حیلہ ناجزہ کی تصنیف کے زمانہ کے مفتیانِ مدینہ منورہ، حضرت علامہ الفا با شم مالکی علامہ مفتی سعید بن صدیق خلاقی، علامہ مفتی محمد طیب الانصاری، مفتی عبداللہ فوتی، و دیگر مالکی مفتیان مسجد نبوی کی خدمت میں ارسال کیا گیا سوال نامہ اور مذکورہ مفتیانِ مالکیہ کے جوابات حسب سابق باقی رکھے گئے ہیں البتہ حیلہ ناجزہ میں حضرت نے مالکیہ کا اردو میں جو مسئلہ بیان فرمایا ہے قدیم نسخہ میں اس کی دلیل عربی فتوے سے کے ساتھ کافی فاصلہ پر درج تھی جس کی نشان دہی حضرت نے روایات کا نمبر تحریر فرما کر فرمائی تھی۔ راقم الحروف نے بعض مقام پر مالکیہ کے مسئلہ کی دلیل ساتھ ہی ساتھ عربی فتوے سے عربی میں ہی پیش کر دی اور سابقہ جگہ بھی وہ عبارت عربی فتوے میں بھی باقی رکھی اور اردو میں بھی اسی جگہ عنوان لگا دیا۔

(۶) جن رسائل کے عربی میں نام تھے وہ قدیم نام بھی باقی رکھے البتہ افادہ عام کی غرض سے تعارفی جدید ناموں کا بھی اضافہ کر دیا جس کی وضاحت فہرست مضامین میں ہے ۔

(۷) "الجبلۃ الناجزہ " پر حین اکابر و علماء ہند نے تصدیقات تحریر فرمائی ہے ان کے اسماء گرامی کی ایک تفصیلی فہرست کتاب کے آغاز میں شریک اشاعت کی گئی ہے ۔

(۸) حیلہ ناجزہ کے پانچوں رسائل سابقہ جگہ باقی رکھے گئے ہیں اس کے پہلے رسالے میں تفویض طلاق کے احکام مفقود الخبر عنین، مجنون سے تفریق شرعی کی صورتیں حسب سابق درج کی گئیں ہیں ۔ اسی طرح رسالہ المختارات فی مہمات التفريق والنجارات میں بالغہ کے فسخ
He cooperated and the scholars of Medina, the Muftis of Medina, in obtaining fatwas and correspondence, Sheikh al-Islam Sayyid Husain Ahmad Madani (may his grave be illuminated) also provided extraordinary guidance. Although many editions of this book have been published, the external beauty of the book and attention to modern headings could not be given properly. Therefore, the writer, while preserving the author's expressions, made minor simplifications at some places and established modern headings for the entire book, and performed the following services in this regard:

(1) For the old edition of al-Majallat al-Najizah, I established modern headings on the expressions of the entire book, compiled a table of contents and a list of headings, and published it.
(2) While preserving the original expressions of the book, I simplified some technical terms, and places where significant simplification was done, I placed them in parentheses, but the author's original meaning has been fully preserved.
(3) In the old edition, at some places the margin note was extremely long, even spanning several pages; so I made it an independent article with a modern heading and placed it at the end of the relevant article, and at such places a brief note was given in the margin so that this new arrangement could be clarified.
(4) In the previous edition, where there was a short margin note, I kept it, but at some places I established a heading for it in the margin, and at some places if the margin note was in Arabic, I presented its meaning in Urdu.

(5) The questionnaire sent to the Muftis of Medina at the time of composition of Hilatun Najizah—namely, the Maliki Mufti Sayyid bin Sadiq Khallaqi, Mufti Muhammad Tayyib al-Ansari, Mufti Abdullah al-Futi, and other Maliki Muftis of the Prophet's Mosque—and the responses of the aforementioned Maliki Muftis have been kept as before. However, in Hilatun Najizah, the author presented the Maliki position in Urdu; in the old edition, its proof was recorded at a considerable distance from the Arabic fatwa, and the author had indicated this by writing the reference number. At some places, I presented the proof of the Maliki position together with the Arabic fatwa in Arabic, and also kept that expression in the Arabic fatwa at its previous place, and also added a heading in Urdu at the same place.

(6) Those treatises that had Arabic names were retained with their old names, but for general benefit, new descriptive names were also added, as clarified in the table of contents.

(7) On al-Jublat al-Najizah, some Indian scholars and ulema have written endorsements; a detailed list of their honorable names has been included at the beginning of the book.

(8) The five treatises of Hilatun Najizah have been kept in their previous places. In the first treatise, the rulings on delegation of divorce (tafwid talaq), cases of a missing husband (mafqud al-khabar), an impotent man (inanin), and legal separation from an insane person (majnoon) have been recorded as before. Similarly, in the treatise al-Mukhtarat fi Muhimmat al-Tafriq wa al-Najarat, the annulment of a mature woman...
Source pages p. 19

Commentary
This passage is the editor's preface, explaining the methodology and revisions made in this new edition of Al-Hilatul Najijah. The editor acknowledges the guidance of Shaykh al-Islam Sayyid Husain Ahmad Madani and the Muftis of Medina. The key editorial interventions include: (1) adding modern headings to the entire text and compiling a table of contents; (2) simplifying technical terms while preserving the original meaning, with notable simplifications placed in parentheses; (3) relocating lengthy marginal notes to the end of relevant articles as independent sections, with a brief margin note indicating the change; (4) retaining short margin notes but sometimes adding headings, and translating Arabic margin notes into Urdu; (5) keeping the original questionnaire and Maliki fatwas, but placing the Arabic proof alongside the Urdu explanation of the Maliki position for clarity; (6) adding new descriptive names in Urdu for treatises that originally had Arabic names; (7) including a list of endorsements from Indian scholars; (8) retaining the five treatises in the same order, with the first treatise covering delegation of divorce, missing husband, impotence, and separation from an insane spouse, and the second treatise (al-Mukhtarat) dealing with annulment for a mature woman.

Key Terms
حیلہ ناجزہ (Hilatun Najizah): The title of the book: 'The Effective Legal Stratagem'
تفویض طلاق (tafwid al-talaq): Delegation of divorce, a legal mechanism where the husband delegates the right to divorce to the wife or a third party.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What did the editor do with the lengthy marginal notes from the old edition?
A) He deleted them entirely.
B) He kept them exactly as they were.
C) He turned them into independent articles with new headings and placed them at the end of the relevant article.
D) He summarized them into brief footnotes.

Key Takeaway
Faithful editing preserves the author's original text while enhancing its accessibility for contemporary readers, a key principle in transmitting Hanafi fatwas.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Parsing an Editorial Introduction in a Fiqh Compilation
Editorial preface detailing modifications in a new edition.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the key editorial changes described in the preface of Al-Hilatun Najijah and state their purpose for the mufti's use of the text.

Core Idea
An editor's preface reveals the textual history and structural choices that affect how a mufti accesses rulings.

When a mufti opens a new edition of a classical fiqh work, the editor's introduction is not mere formality. It documents decisions about layout, language, and content that directly impact the reliability and usability of the text. This lesson walks you through the preface of Al-Hilatun Najijah to understand what changed and why.

Guided Path
1
Identify the editorial voice
Recognize that the passage is written by 'Raqim al-Huruf' (the editor), not the original author Ashraf Ali Thanwi. This helps distinguish the core content from editorial additions.
In Hanafi works, later editions often include such editorial prefaces.
2
Categorize the changes
List the types of changes: preservation of original content, improvement of layout (placing proofs alongside), addition of descriptive titles, moving endorsements, and including practical legal documents. Each has a distinct purpose for the mufti.
Use the Arabic text to identify each change.
3
Note the cross-madhhab element
The editor kept the Maliki fatwa questionnaire and responses, showing that the work incorporates Maliki opinions for legal stratagems. This is significant for muftis dealing with cross-madhhab cases.
The editor did not remove or alter the Maliki content.
4
Recognize the practical addition
The editor added court documents based on his experience at Darul Qadha. This transforms the book from a theoretical work to a practical manual for muftis.
These additions are part of the editor's own contribution.
5
Evaluate editorial humility
The editor acknowledges possible errors and requests correction. This reminds the mufti to verify crucial information, even in a well-edited text.
Standard scholarly practice but important for the mufti's caution.

(۵) حیلہ ناجزہ کی تصنیف کے زمانہ کے مفتیانِ مدینہ منورہ، حضرت علامہ الفا با شم مالکی علامہ مفتی سعید بن صدیق خلاقی، علامہ مفتی محمد طیب الانصاری، مفتی عبداللہ فوتی، و دیگر مالکی مفتیان مسجد نبوی کی خدمت میں ارسال کیا گیا سوال نامہ اور مذکورہ مفتیانِ مانکیہ کے جوابات حسب سابق باقی رکھے گئے ہیں البتہ حیلہ ناجزہ میں حضرت نے مالکیہ کا اردو میں جو مسئلہ بیان فرمایا ہے قدیم نسخہ میں اس کی دلیل عربی فتواسے کے ساتھ کافی فاصلہ پر درج تھی جس کی نشان دہی حضرت نے روایات کا نمبر تحریر فرما کر فرمائی تھی۔ راقم الحروف نے بعض مقام پر مالکیہ کے مسئلہ کی دلیل ساتھ ہی ساتھ عربی فتوئی سے عربی میں ہی پیش کر دی اور سابقہ جگہ بھی وہ عبارت عربی فتوے میں بھی باقی رکھی اور اردو میں بھی اُسی جگہ عنوان لگا دیا۔
جن رسائل کے عربی میں نام تھے وہ قدیم نام بھی باقی رکھے البتہ افادہ عام کی غرض سے تعارفی جدید ناموں کا بھی اضافہ کر دیا جس کی وضاحت فہرست مضامین میں ہے ۔
(۷) "الجبلۃ الناجزہ " پر حین اکابر و علماء ہند نے تصدیقات تحریر فرمائی ہے ان کے اسماء گرامی کی ایک تفصیلی فہرست کتاب کے آغاز میں شریک اشاعت کی گئی ہے ۔
(۸) جیلہ ناجزہ کے پانچوں رسائل سابقہ جگہ باقی رکھے گئے ہیں اس کے پہلے رسالے میں تفویض طلاق کے احکام مفقود الخبر عنین، مجنون سے تفریق شرعی کی صورتیں حسب سابق درج کی گئیں ہیں ۔
اسی طرح رسالہ المختارات فی مہمات التفريق والنجارات میں بالغہ کے فسخ نکاح کی تفصیلی بحث اور حرمت مصاہرت کے احکام، کفور، غیر کفو میں نکاج کی بحث پیش کی گئی ہے ۔
(۹) اور رسالہ حکم الازدواج میں غیر مسلم اقوام اور یورپین اقوام سے نکاح کے احکام بیان کیے گئے ہیں اور سابقہ نسخہ کی طرح ریسا لہ المرقومات للمظلومات میں مذکورہ تمام رسائل کا عام فہم خلاصہ پیش کیا گیا ہے نیز رفاق المجتہدین نے وفاق المجتہدین یں تحیلہ ناجزہ پر پیش کئے گئے سوالات اور حیلہ ناجزہ پر کیے گئے شبہات کا جامع جواب پیش کیا گیا ہے ۔
مادر علمی دارالعلوم دیوبند میں از سه تا ته چھ سال تک محکمہ عدلیہ و تا سایہ چھ شرعیہ دارالقضاء کے قیام کے دوران راقم الحروف کو بطور معتمد دار القضاء جو خدمات کا موقعہ ملا اور مختلف نوعیت کے جو شرعی مقدمات سامنے آئے۔ ان تجربات کی روشنی میں مدعی / مدعا علیہ کو نوٹس روانہ کرنے کا مضمون مختار نامہ ثالث نامہ کا مضمون اور شرعی مقدمہ کی سرکاری حیثیت بنانے سے متعلق جیه رہنمائی پیشتمل مسودات اور عرضی دعوئی، درخواست دعوئی کا مسودہ وغیرہ بھی شریک اشاعت کیا گیا ۔
(۱۰) مدرسہ نظاہر العلوم سہارن پور، خانقاہ امدادیہ تھانہ بھون، دیوبندی دہلی کے مفتیان کرام اور دیگر اکابر علما ہند کی جو تصدیقات قدیم نسخے میں آغاز کتاب میں شامل تھیں ان کو آخر کتاب میں شریک اشاعت کیا گیا ۔ مذکورہ تمام امور کی انجام دہی میں غیر معمولی احتیاط سے کام لیا گیا، پھر بھی سهو و نسیان خارج از امکان نہیں۔ اس لیے جو سہو نظر سے گزرے از راه نوازش راقم الحروف کو مطلع فرمائیں تا کہ آئندہ اس کی اصلاح کی جاسکے۔
(5) The questionnaire sent to the Muftis of Madinah Munawwarah at the time of the composition of Hilatun Najijah – Hadhrat Allamah al-Fa ... Maliki, Allamah Mufti Sa'id bin Siddiq Khallaqi, Allamah Mufti Muhammad Tayyib al-Ansari, Mufti Abdullah Futi, and other Maliki Muftis of the Prophet's Mosque – and the answers of the mentioned Maliki Muftis have been kept as before. However, in Hilatun Najijah, the issue that Hadhrat explained in Urdu concerning the Malikis, in the old edition its proof was placed at a considerable distance from the Arabic fatwa, and Hadhrat had indicated it by writing the number of the narration. The editor has, at some places, presented the proof of the Maliki issue alongside the Arabic fatwa in Arabic itself, and also kept that text in the earlier place in the Arabic fatwa, and added a title in Urdu at that same place. (6) For those treatises that had Arabic names, the old names were retained, but for general benefit, new descriptive names were added, as clarified in the table of contents. (7) The endorsements written by senior scholars of India on "al-Hilatun Najijah" – a detailed list of their noble names has been included at the beginning of the book. (8) All five treatises of Hilatun Najijah have been kept in their previous places. In the first treatise, the rulings on delegation of divorce (tafwid al-talaq), the missing husband (mafqud al-khabar), the impotent ('innin), and the forms of judicial separation from a madman (majnun) have been recorded as before. Similarly, in the treatise al-Mukhtarat fi Muhimmat al-Tafriq wa al-Najarat, a detailed discussion of the annulment of marriage by a mature woman, the rulings on the prohibition of affinity (hurmat al-musaharat), and the discussion of marriage with a non-equivalent (ghayr kufu') have been presented. (9) And in the treatise Hukm al-Izdawaj, the rulings on marriage with non-Muslim nations and European nations are explained, and, like the previous edition, in Risalah al-Marqumat li al-Mazlumat, a summary of all the mentioned treatises in common language is presented. Also, Rafiq al-Mujtahidin has presented a comprehensive response to the questions raised on Hilatun Najijah and the doubts made about it in Wifaq al-Mujtahidin. (10) The endorsements that were included at the beginning of the old edition from Madrasa Nazahir al-Ulum Saharanpur, Khanqah Imdadiyya Thana Bhawan, Deobandi Delhi's esteemed Muftis, and other senior scholars of India have been moved to the end of the book. In carrying out all the above tasks, extraordinary caution was exercised, yet error and forgetfulness are not beyond possibility. Therefore, if any mistake escapes notice, kindly inform the editor as a favor, so that it may be corrected in the future.
Source pages p. 20

Commentary
This passage is the editor's (raqim al-huruf) preface explaining the changes and additions made in the new edition of Hilatun Najijah. The editor describes preserving the original questionnaire and responses from Maliki muftis of Madinah, but improving the layout by placing Arabic proofs alongside the Urdu statements. Arabic-named treatises retain their old names but gain new descriptive titles for wider accessibility. Endorsements from Indian scholars are now listed at the start. The five original treatises remain unchanged, covering topics like tafwid al-talaq, missing husband, impotence, judicial separation from a madman, annulment of marriage by a mature woman, prohibitions of affinity, marriage with non-equivalents, and marriage with non-Muslims. A summary treatise and a response to questions and doubts are included. Additionally, based on the editor's experience at Darul Uloom Deoband's shariah court, practical legal documents like notices to litigants, appointment of arbitrators, and plaint drafts are added. The endorsements have been moved to the end. The editor acknowledges the possibility of errors and requests readers to inform him for future correction.

Key Terms
حیلہ ناجزہ (Hilatun Najijah): The title of this book by Ashraf Ali Thanwi, meaning 'The Effective Legal Stratagem'.
راقم الحروف (Raqim al-Huruf): The editor or scribe who compiled and annotated this edition.
تفویض طلاق (Tafwid al-Talaq): Delegation of the power to divorce to the wife or a third party.

Key Terms from Source Passage

B) Al-Mukhtarat fi Muhimmat al-Tafriq wa al-Najarat
C) Risalah al-Marqumat
D) Wifaq al-Mujtahidin

Key Takeaway
The preface helps the mufti navigate the edition and understand its structural improvements, ensuring correct use of the text.

The Comprehensive Methodology of a Hanafi Iftaa Compilation
Author lists supplementary contents and updates in the new edition

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the key components of a Hanafi iftaa collection and explain how a mufti's practical experience enriches his fatwa compilation.

Core Idea
A complete Hanafi fatwa collection integrates core jurisprudence, contemporary issues, procedural documents, and scholarly endorsements.

The author of Al-Hilatul Najizah, after presenting the classical Hanafi rulings on marriage and related topics, uses this afterword to detail the supplementary materials he included in this edition. This lesson walks you through those components, showing how a mufti systematically documents his rulings and supports them with practical tools.

Guided Path
1
Identify the main topics added
List the core fiqh topics mentioned: nikah (marriage), musaharat (prohibition by marriage), kafa'ah (equality in marriage), and marriage with non-Muslims.
These are not just abstract rulings; they address contemporary needs, such as marriage with European nations.
2
Recognize the supplementary treatises
Note the three treatises included: Hukm al-Izdawaj (on marriage with non-Muslims), Risala al-Marqumat lil-Mazlumat (summary of previous treatises), and Rafaq al-Mujtahidin (responses to doubts on Hila Najiza).
Each treatise serves a distinct purpose: contemporary application, summarization, and defense of the core work.
3
Understand the inclusion of procedural documents
The author draws on his experience as a trusted representative of Dar al-Qada to provide sample drafts for legal documents (notice, power of attorney, plaint).
This bridges theory and practice, showing how a mufti equips users to implement rulings in a court setting.
4
Note the rearrangement of endorsements
Scholarly endorsements, previously at the beginning, are now placed at the end.
This reflects a common editorial choice to prioritize the main content while retaining scholarly validation.
5
Reflect on the author's caution and humility
The author acknowledges potential errors and invites corrections, demonstrating the ethical responsibility of a mufti-compiler.
This aligns with the adab al-mufti principle of thoroughness and openness to critique.
